<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:экологически.html>экологи́чески</a> (18294)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:экологический.html>экологи́ческий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ekologíčeskij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:соорудить.html>-и</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-i</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:экологически.html>экологи́чески</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ekologíčeski</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>ecologically, environmentally
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:экологически.html>экологи́чески</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:чистый.html>чи́стый</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ekologíčeski</b> čístyj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">environmentally safe/appropriate; clean; pollution-free</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:экологически.html>экологи́чески</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:приемлемый.html>прие́млемый</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ekologíčeski</b> prijémlemyj</i> ― <span class="e-translation">environmentally friendly/sound</span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:экономить.html>эконо́мить</a> (9022)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:экономия.html>эконо́мия</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ekonómija</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-ить</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-itʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:экономить.html>эконо́мить</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ekonómitʹ</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="imperfective aspect">impf</abbr></span> (<i>perfective</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сэкономить.html>сэконо́мить</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>to save
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:экономить.html>эконо́мить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:время.html>вре́мя</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ekonómitʹ</b> vrémja</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to save time</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:экономить.html>эконо́мить</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:на.html>на</a> чём-либо</i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ekonómitʹ</b> na čóm-libo</i> ― <span class="e-translation">to save on something, to spend less on something</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li>to economize <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">imperfective only</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:сэкономить.html>сэконо́мить</a></span> <span class="gender"><abbr title="perfective aspect">pf</abbr></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">sɛkonómitʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>

***экономический.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:экономический.html>экономи́ческий</a> (1175)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:эконом.html>эконо́м</a>(ика)</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ekonóm(ika)</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ческий</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-íčeskij</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:экономический.html>экономи́ческий</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ekonomíčeskij</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>economic <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">relating to the economy</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:экономический.html>экономи́ческий</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:кризис.html>кри́зис</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ekonomíčeskij</b> krízis</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>economic</b> crisis</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> economical, thrifty</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Not to be confused with <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:экономный.html>эконо́мный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ekonómnyj</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">economical, thrifty</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:экономичный.html>экономи́чный</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ekonomíčnyj</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">economical, efficient</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li></ul>

<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:частичный.html>части́чный</a>: <a href = vnd.unilang:хозяйственный.html>хозя́йственный</a></li></ol>

***экономичный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:экономичный.html>экономи́чный</a> (30996)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:экономия.html>эконо́мия</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ekonómija</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́чный</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-íčnyj</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:экономичный.html>экономи́чный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ekonomíčnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>economical in terms of efficiency, efficient
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:экономичный.html>экономи́чный</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:автомобиль.html>автомоби́ль</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ekonomíčnyj</b> avtomobílʹ</i> ― <span class="e-translation">an <b>economical</b> automobile</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:экономичный.html>экономи́чное</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:мыло.html>мы́ло</a></i> ― <i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>ekonomíčnoje</b> mýlo</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><b>economical</b> soap <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">a <a href = vnd.unilang:бар.html>bar</a> of soap that can be used for a long time</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></span></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Not to be confused with <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:экономический.html>экономи́ческий</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">ekonomíčeskij</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">relational</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> (local, national, or worldwide) economy; economic</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:экономия.html>эконо́мия</a> (8203)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:экономия.html>эконо́мия</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ekonómija</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:экономия.html>эконо́мии</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:экономия.html>эконо́мии</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:экономия.html>эконо́мий</a></b>)

***экскурсия.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:экскурсия.html>экску́рсия</a> (6304)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">excursio</i>, through the intermediate of another language.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:экскурсия.html>экску́рсия</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">ekskúrsija</span>) <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr> <abbr title="inanimate">inan</abbr></span> (<i>genitive</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:экскурсия.html>экску́рсии</a></b>, <i>nominative plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:экскурсия.html>экску́рсии</a></b>, <i>genitive plural</i> <b class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:экскурсия.html>экску́рсий</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>excursion, outing, hiking <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">brief recreational trip</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span></li></ol>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:эксперимент.html>экспериме́нт</a> (3038)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">experīmentum</i>.

***экспериментальный.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:экспериментальный.html>эксперимента́льный</a> (9672)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Cyrl headword" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:экспериментальный.html>эксперимента́льный</a></strong> • (<span lang="ru-Latn" class="headword-tr manual-tr tr Latn" dir="ltr">eksperimentálʹnyj</span>)
</p>
<ol><li>experimental
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Cyrl mention e-example" lang="ru"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:экспериментальный.html>эксперимента́льная</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:физика.html>фи́зика</a> — <a href = vnd.unilang:способ.html>спо́соб</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:познание.html>позна́ния</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:природа.html>приро́ды</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:заключаться.html>заключа́ющийся</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:изучение.html>изуче́нии</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:природный.html>приро́дных</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:явление.html>явле́ний</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:в.html>в</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:специальный.html>специа́льно</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:приготовленный.html>пригото́вленных</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:условие.html>усло́виях</a>.</i><dl><dd><i lang="ru-Latn" class="e-transliteration tr Latn"><b>Eksperimentálʹnaja</b> fízika — spósob poznánija priródy, zaključájuščijsja v izučénii priródnyx javlénij v speciálʹno prigotóvlennyx uslóvijax.</i></dd><dd><span class="e-translation"><b>Experimental physics</b> - a way of cognition of nature, which consists in the study of natural phenomena in a specially prepared environment.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Related_terms">Related terms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Cyrl" lang="ru"><a href = vnd.unilang:эксперимент.html>экспериме́нт</a></span> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="tr Latn">eksperimént</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span id=".D0.97.D0.BD.D0.B0.D1.87.D0.B5.D0.BD.D0.B8.D0.B5"></span><span class="mw-headline" id="Значение"><a href = vnd.unilang:значение.html>Значе́ние</a></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:экспериментировать.html>эксперименти́ровать</a> (22044)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">experimentieren</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">experimentare</i>. For the suffix, see <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">-и́ровать</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">-írovatʹ</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
